name:F‚ÄçG‚ÄçT‚ÄçR‚ÄçT‚ÄçD
info:Superior King Room
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Business travelers
info:10 Reviews
rating:2
posted:Posted January 26, 2023
msg:Positives: 
The staff tries hard.
Negatives: 
The spa was closed. 
The 2nd floor bar has been closed for a year but advertising for it is still all over the hotel. 
Other than the buffet (which was too busy due to it being spring festival) the only other dining options were the lobby bar or room service. 
The lobby bar closes at 8pm and there's nothing else within a walkable distance to make up for the lack of options in the hotel. 
Room service food was edible but not worth it.You have to go downstairs to receive food deliveries. 
The kettle plug didn't fit the outlet. 
The bathroom was a little dirty. 
My breakfast card wasn't picked up overnight. They made up for this by comping my breakfast. Again, edible.

All in all I think the hotel has been hit hard by covid and they're not able to keep the standards you'd expect. I'd have been better off at a self service apartment. At least then deliveries would arrive to my door.
----------------------------------------

name:J‚ÄçM
info:Superior Room (2 beds)
info:Stayed in January 2023
info:Family
info:4 Reviews
rating:5
posted:Posted January 31, 2023
msg:Location of the hotel is perfect for people coming from Hong Kong by metro (Futian border crossing), it's at less than 10 minutes walking distance. And although the surrounding of the hotel is in some kind of a trading zone, and you can't avoid passing by big storage areas when walking, you wouldn't feel it when going by car.
Our room was spacious and clean, and breakfast buffet was very good! People working in all areas of the hotel are warm and friendly, and there was always someone in the lobby who could speak English.
Right beside the hotel, there is a nice spa for those who want to relax.
I am quite satisfied with the hotel and I believe I will stay here every time I need to commute between Shenzhen and Hong Kong in future!

It turns out that the hotel is divided into two buildings. We asked not to use a bathtub, so we were assigned a room on the 22nd floor of the west building. To get to the west building, we have to go through a long corridor from the 5th floor to get there, but basically at night There was no pedestrian traffic, and there was a door leading to a commercial building, but there were no lights on at the time. The location was quite dark and scary, so I asked the hotel staff to accompany me along this corridor. Ôøº

However, the experience in the hotel lobby is completely different from that in the room. The hotel is relatively old and different from the newer hotels now. It seems that the hotel really needs to be improved. Then we purchased this package which included dinner buffet and breakfast. Dinner was really scary. We went to eat at about 7:00. The food turned out to be sweet potatoes, corn, whole grains, and the poor food was not as good as what I saw online. Then I asked the waiter why he gave such food. It turned out Because there are tour groups, the food for the tour group is different from what we saved, and we were told that the food will be richer after 7:30. At this time, the food is really different. There are oysters, stewed soup, foie gras toast, and more frozen seafood. However, the seafood is really not frozen enough. I don‚Äôt think it is ideal. At breakfast, there are also group guests, so The overall restaurant experience was not very good, and the breakfast food was just average. So I left the hotel early and will not stay in this hotel again next time. Although it is a brand, I have stayed in Shanghai and Taiwan. Compared with this time, the experience is really not good.
